1 自然地理

lithosphere|n.|岩石圈|The hydrosphere and the lithosphere together form the earth's surface
---

7 文化历史
+++
culture|n.|文化；文明；教养|China plays an important role in promoting Asian culture|cultural adj. 文化的。multicultural adj. 文化多样的

renaissance|n.|the Renaissance 文艺复兴时期|The Renaissance was an epoch of unparalleled cultural achievement 文艺复兴时期是一个在文化上取得空前成就的时代|epoch n. （尤指出现新进步和大变革的）时代，纪元，时期——注意美音和英音的发音区别。unparalleled adj. 无双的，无比的，空前的

ideology|n.|意识形态；思想体系|An obsolete ideology can hamper an economy|obsolete adj. 废弃的，过时的，老化的，淘汰的。hamper v./n. 阻碍，妨碍/带盖的方形大容器，食品盒，洗衣篮

---

---
exotic|adj.|外来的；异国情调的|The exotic atmosphere will fascinate you

alien|n./adj.|外侨；外星人；外国的；陌生的|I ran into an old friend in the alien land. 他乡遇故知|run into sb./sth. 偶然遇到、无意碰见（某人）/遇到、陷入（困境）；共计，合计。  alienate v. 使疏远；使不友好；离间。an alien culture 异域文化
anthropologist|n.|人类学家|The anthropologist contrasted two cultures in his lecture. 这位人类学家在讲座中将两种文化进行对比|contrast v./n. 对比，对照/差异，对照物，（屏幕、显示器）对比度。anthropology n. 人类学

---
thrive|v.|繁荣；兴旺发达；茁壮成长|First thrive and then wive. 先立业，后成家|wive v. 娶妻

setback|n.|挫折；阻碍|This setback has drained away my keenness|drain sth. away （使）彻底消失;（使）流失。keenness n. 积极；敏锐，精明；渴望，热衷；锋利
adversity|n.|逆境|Hardship disposes man to meet adversity. 困苦使人们愿意去客户困境|dispose sb. to/towards sb./sth. 表示使某人对某人或某事物产生一种倾向、态度或情感。

oral|adj.|口头的|Students of English should have a lot of oral drills|drill n. 钻头，（尤指军事）练习 a spelling/pronunciation drill 拼写／发音练习
